<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预测模型未能充分利用电子健康记录（EHR）中的多模态（文本、实验室检查、时间序列）和时间信息，导致预测慢性病时效果不佳，因此需要一个能够整合这些复杂数据源以提高预测精度的模型。

Method: CURENet模型结合了两种主要技术：1. 利用大型语言模型（LLM）处理非结构化临床笔记和文本化的实验室检查结果。2. 利用Transformer编码器处理患者随时间变化的时间序列就诊数据。通过融合这两种模态的处理结果，模型能够捕捉不同数据类型之间的交互作用。

Result: 在MIMIC-III和FEMH两个数据集上，CURENet在多标签框架下预测十大慢性病的准确率均超过94%，证明了其在整合多模态EHR数据方面的有效性。

Conclusion: CURENet模型通过有效整合电子健康记录中的多模态和时间序列数据，显著提高了慢性病的预测准确性。这一成果展示了多模态EHR整合在辅助临床决策和改善患者预后方面的巨大潜力，为未来开发更精准的医疗预测模型提供了方向。

Abstract: Electronic health records (EHRs) are designed to synthesize diverse data types, including unstructured clinical notes, structured lab tests, and time-series visit data. Physicians draw on these multimodal and temporal sources of EHR data to form a comprehensive view of a patient's health, which is crucial for informed therapeutic decision-making. Yet, most predictive models fail to fully capture the interactions, redundancies, and temporal patterns across multiple data modalities, often focusing on a single data type or overlooking these complexities. In this paper, we present CURENet, a multimodal model (Combining Unified Representations for Efficient chronic disease prediction) that integrates unstructured clinical notes, lab tests, and patients' time-series data by utilizing large language models (LLMs) for clinical text processing and textual lab tests, as well as transformer encoders for longitudinal sequential visits. CURENet has been capable of capturing the intricate interaction between different forms of clinical data and creating a more reliable predictive model for chronic illnesses. We evaluated CURENet using the public MIMIC-III and private FEMH datasets, where it achieved over 94\% accuracy in predicting the top 10 chronic conditions in a multi-label framework. Our findings highlight the potential of multimodal EHR integration to enhance clinical decision-making and improve patient outcomes.

### [104] [Experience-Guided Adaptation of Inference-Time Reasoning Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11519)
*Adam Stein,Matthew Trager,Benjamin Bowman,Michael Kleinman,Aditya Chattopadhyay,Wei Xia,Stefano Soatto*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Experience-Guided Reasoner (EGuR) is a novel agentic AI system that dynamically generates tailored problem-solving strategies at inference time, adapting all components including prompts, sampling parameters, and tool configurations. This approach significantly improves accuracy (up to 14%) and reduces computational costs (up to 111x) across challenging benchmarks compared to existing methods, with performance gains increasing with accumulated experience.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing agentic AI systems struggle to adapt their problem-solving strategies after initial training, particularly when needing to modify parameters beyond simple textual input. Systems that do offer more flexible adaptation often require costly offline optimization and become static once deployed. This limitation hinders their ability to efficiently tackle diverse and complex problems that benefit from dynamic adjustments to their computational procedures.

Method: EGuR introduces a two-component system: a Guide and a Consolidator. The Guide, an LLM-based meta-strategy generator, creates multiple candidate strategies (including LLM calls, tool usage, sampling parameters, and control logic) based on the current problem and a structured memory of past experiences. The Consolidator refines future strategy generation by integrating feedback from strategy execution. This allows for the dynamic, real-time generation of complete computational procedures, optimizing all aspects of the strategy.

Result: EGuR demonstrated significant improvements across five challenging benchmarks (AIME 2025, 3-SAT, and three Big Bench Extra Hard tasks). It achieved accuracy improvements of up to 14% over the strongest baselines and reduced computational costs by up to 111x. Notably, both accuracy and efficiency metrics continued to improve as EGuR accumulated more experience, highlighting its adaptive learning capabilities.

Conclusion: EGuR represents a significant advancement in creating adaptable agentic AI systems. By enabling dynamic strategy generation at inference time, it overcomes the limitations of static or input-limited adaptation methods. The system

Abstract: Enabling agentic AI systems to adapt their problem-solving approaches based on post-training interactions remains a fundamental challenge. While systems that update and maintain a memory at inference time have been proposed, existing designs only steer the system by modifying textual input to a language model or agent, which means that they cannot change sampling parameters, remove tools, modify system prompts, or switch between agentic and workflow paradigms. On the other hand, systems that adapt more flexibly require offline optimization and remain static once deployed. We present Experience-Guided Reasoner (EGuR), which generates tailored strategies -- complete computational procedures involving LLM calls, tools, sampling parameters, and control logic -- dynamically at inference time based on accumulated experience. We achieve this using an LLM-based meta-strategy -- a strategy that outputs strategies -- enabling adaptation of all strategy components (prompts, sampling parameters, tool configurations, and control logic). EGuR operates through two components: a Guide generates multiple candidate strategies conditioned on the current problem and structured memory of past experiences, while a Consolidator integrates execution feedback to improve future strategy generation. This produces complete, ready-to-run strategies optimized for each problem, which can be cached, retrieved, and executed as needed without wasting resources. Across five challenging benchmarks (AIME 2025, 3-SAT, and three Big Bench Extra Hard tasks), EGuR achieves up to 14% accuracy improvements over the strongest baselines while reducing computational costs by up to 111x, with both metrics improving as the system gains experience.

</details>

Abstract: Ever since the vision was formulated, the Semantic Web has inspired many generations of innovations. Semantic technologies have been used to share vast amounts of information on the Web, enhance them with semantics to give them meaning, and enable inference and reasoning on them. Throughout the years, semantic technologies, and in particular knowledge graphs, have been used in search engines, data integration, enterprise settings, and machine learning. In this paper, we recap the classical concepts and foundations of the Semantic Web as well as modern and recent concepts and applications, building upon these foundations. We conclude with an outlook on the future directions of the Semantic Web.

### [106] [CoEvo: Continual Evolution of Symbolic Solutions Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2412.18890)
*Ping Guo,Qingfu Zhang,Xi Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了CoEvo框架，一种结合大型语言模型（LLM）和进化搜索的新方法，用于持续生成和优化符号解决方案。与传统方法和纯粹基于LLM的方法不同，CoEvo通过动态知识库和多表示形式（自然语言、数学表达式、代码）提高了搜索效率和开放式创新能力。实验证明，CoEvo不仅提高了搜索效率，还能支持类似人类科学探索的持续发现过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的符号解决方案（如数学表达式、逻辑规则）的发现方法在搜索效率和知识整合方面存在不足。虽然基于LLM的方法提高了搜索效率，但缺乏持续改进和扩展解决方案及其知识的能力，限制了开放式创新。这阻碍了科学和工程的进步。

Method: CoEvo框架结合了LLM的推理能力和进化算法的探索能力。它利用LLM在一个进化搜索框架内生成和优化符号解决方案，并整合了一个动态知识库以支持开放式创新。此外，CoEvo使用多种解决方案表示形式（自然语言、数学表达式、代码）来提高搜索效率。

Result: 实验结果表明，CoEvo方法显著提高了符号解决方案的搜索效率和发现范围。该方法支持持续的发现过程，类似于人类的科学探索，证明了其在促进科学和工程突破方面的潜力。

Conclusion: CoEvo框架通过结合LLM和进化搜索，并引入动态知识库和多表示形式，成功解决了传统符号解决方案发现方法的局限性。该研究将符号解决方案的搜索视为一个持续的、迭代的过程，为利用LLM推动科学和工程的不断进步提供了新的途径。

Abstract: The discovery of symbolic solutions -- mathematical expressions, logical rules, and algorithmic structures -- is fundamental to advancing scientific and engineering progress.
  However, traditional methods often struggle with search efficiency and fail to integrate knowledge effectively.
  While recent large language model-based (LLM-based) approaches have demonstrated improvements in search efficiency, they lack the ability to continually refine and expand upon discovered solutions and their underlying knowledge, limiting their potential for open-ended innovation.
  To address these limitations, we introduce CoEvo, a novel framework that leverages large language models within an evolutionary search methodology to continually generate and refine symbolic solutions. CoEvo integrates a dynamic knowledge library, enabling open-ended innovation of solutions through effective knowledge management. Additionally, CoEvo leverages multiple representations of solutions -- including natural language, mathematical expressions, and code -- to further enhance search efficiency.
  By combining the reasoning capabilities of LLMs with the exploratory power of evolutionary algorithms, CoEvo significantly improves the efficiency and scope of symbolic discovery.
  Our experimental results demonstrate that this method not only enhances the efficiency of searching for symbolic solutions but also supports the ongoing discovery process, akin to human scientific endeavors. This study represents a first effort in conceptualizing the search for symbolic solutions as a lifelong, iterative
  process, marking a significant step towards harnessing LLMs in the perpetual pursuit of scientific and engineering breakthroughs.
  Our code is available at https://github.com/pgg3/CoEvo.

</details>


### [107] [Sensory-Motor Control with Large Language Models via Iterative Policy Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.04867)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所提出的方法成功地使大型语言模型（LLMs）能够通过生成直接映射连续观测向量到连续动作向量的控制策略来控制具身智能体。该方法通过结合文本描述、迭代学习以及符号与子符号数据的融合，在多种控制任务上取得了最优或接近最优的结果，证明了其在具身智能领域的潜力。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的任务、更大规模的模型以及更高效的学习机制。

Abstract: We propose a method that enables large language models (LLMs) to control embodied agents through the generation of control policies that directly map continuous observation vectors to continuous action vectors. At the outset, the LLMs generate a control strategy based on a textual description of the agent, its environment, and the intended goal. This strategy is then iteratively refined through a learning process in which the LLMs are repeatedly prompted to improve the current strategy, using performance feedback and sensory-motor data collected during its evaluation. The method is validated on classic control tasks from the Gymnasium library and the inverted pendulum task from the MuJoCo library. The approach proves effective with relatively compact models such as GPT-oss:120b and Qwen2.5:72b. In most cases, it successfully identifies optimal or near-optimal solutions by integrating symbolic knowledge derived through reasoning with sub-symbolic sensory-motor data gathered as the agent interacts with its environment.

Abstract: Representing the temporal evolution of legal norms is a critical challenge for automated processing. This paper proposes a structured, temporal modeling pattern grounded in the LRMoo ontology. The legislative amendment process is formalized through event-centric modeling, allowing changes to be traced precisely. This provides a verifiable semantic backbone for legal knowledge graphs, offering a deterministic foundation for trustworthy legal AI.

### [109] [MUDAS: Mote-scale Unsupervised Domain Adaptation in Multi-label Sound Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.11331)
*Jihoon Yun,Chengzhang Li,Dhrubojyoti Roy,Anish Arora*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MUDAS是一个为资源受限的物联网环境设计的无监督域自适应（UDA）框架，用于多标签声音分类。它通过选择性地在原位使用高置信度数据重新训练分类器来高效地适应模型，从而最大限度地减少计算和内存需求，适用于设备部署。MUDAS还包括特定类别的自适应阈值以生成可靠的伪标签，并应用多样性正则化来提高多标签分类准确性。在SONYC-UST数据集上的评估表明，MUDAS在资源受限的物联网环境中比现有的UDA算法在分类准确性方面有了显著提高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MUDAS框架通过选择性地在原位使用高置信度数据重新训练分类器来高效地适应模型，最大限度地减少计算和内存需求，以适应设备部署。此外，MUDAS还结合了特定类别的自适应阈值来生成可靠的伪标签，并应用多样性正则化来提高多标签分类准确性。在SONYC-UST数据集上进行了评估。

Result: 在SONYC-UST数据集上，MUDAS在资源受限的物联网环境中取得了显著的分类准确性改进，并且在性能上优于现有的UDA算法。

Conclusion: MUDAS是一个高效的UDA框架，专门为资源受限的物联网环境中的多标签声音分类而设计。它通过选择性重训练、自适应阈值和多样性正则化，在计算和内存效率方面取得了显著的性能提升，能够应对真实世界的挑战，如城市声音分类。

Abstract: Unsupervised Domain Adaptation (UDA) is essential for adapting machine learning models to new, unlabeled environments where data distribution shifts can degrade performance. Existing UDA algorithms are designed for single-label tasks and rely on significant computational resources, limiting their use in multi-label scenarios and in resource-constrained IoT devices. Overcoming these limitations is particularly challenging in contexts such as urban sound classification, where overlapping sounds and varying acoustics require robust, adaptive multi-label capabilities on low-power, on-device systems. To address these limitations, we introduce Mote-scale Unsupervised Domain Adaptation for Sounds (MUDAS), a UDA framework developed for multi-label sound classification in resource-constrained IoT settings. MUDAS efficiently adapts models by selectively retraining the classifier in situ using high-confidence data, minimizing computational and memory requirements to suit on-device deployment. Additionally, MUDAS incorporates class-specific adaptive thresholds to generate reliable pseudo-labels and applies diversity regularization to improve multi-label classification accuracy. In evaluations on the SONYC Urban Sound Tagging (SONYC-UST) dataset recorded at various New York City locations, MUDAS demonstrates notable improvements in classification accuracy over existing UDA algorithms, achieving good performance in a resource-constrained IoT setting.

### [110] [Comprehension Without Competence: Architectural Limits of LLMs in Symbolic Computation and Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.10624)
*Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）在需要符号推理、算术准确性和逻辑一致性的任务中存在系统性缺陷，尽管它们表面流畅。本文通过结构性诊断揭示了“理解”与“能力”之间的持续差距，并将此现象称为计算‘裂脑综合征’，即指令和执行路径在几何和功能上分离。这种局限性普遍存在于数学运算和关系推理等领域，导致模型行为脆弱。研究认为LLM是强大的模式补全引擎，但缺乏原则性、组合式推理的架构支持。研究结果区分了当前LLM的能力边界，并为未来具有元认知控制、原则提升和结构化执行能力的模型提供了方向，同时也解释了可解释性研究的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）虽然在语言流畅性方面表现出色，但在符号推理、算术准确性和逻辑一致性等任务上却系统性地失败。这种“理解”与“能力”之间的差距，以及模型在面对需要精确执行指令的任务时表现出的脆弱性，是亟待解决的关键问题，直接影响了LLM在复杂应用中的可靠性和有效性。

Method: 通过进行对照实验和架构分析，研究人员深入探究了LLM在执行符号推理、算术运算和逻辑一致性任务时的失败机制。具体方法包括但不限于：1. 设计特定任务来隔离和测试模型的推理和执行能力；2. 分析模型内部的计算过程，寻找指令理解与实际执行之间的脱节；3. 跨领域（如数学和关系推理）验证所发现的局限性。

Result: 研究发现，LLM在很多情况下能够正确阐述原则，但却无法可靠地应用它们，这种失败源于计算执行的缺陷而非知识获取的不足。这种现象被称为计算‘裂脑综合征’，因为指令和执行路径在几何和功能上是分离的。这种局限性在数学运算和关系推理等领域普遍存在，解释了为何即使在理想的提示下，模型的行为仍然很脆弱。

Conclusion: LLM本质上是强大的模式补全引擎，但缺乏实现原则性、组合式推理所需的架构支持。本文的研究结果明确了当前LLM能力的界限，并为未来构建具有元认知控制、原则提升和结构化执行能力的模型指明了方向。此外，该诊断还有助于解释为何机器学习可解释性研究的结果可能反映的是训练特定的模式协调，而非通用的计算原则，并揭示了指令与执行路径之间几何分离所带来的神经内省和机制分析的局限性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) display striking surface fluency yet systematically fail at tasks requiring symbolic reasoning, arithmetic accuracy, and logical consistency. This paper offers a structural diagnosis of such failures, revealing a persistent gap between \textit{comprehension} and \textit{competence}. Through controlled experiments and architectural analysis, we demonstrate that LLMs often articulate correct principles without reliably applying them--a failure rooted not in knowledge access, but in computational execution. We term this phenomenon the computational \textit{split-brain syndrome}, where instruction and action pathways are geometrically and functionally dissociated. This core limitation recurs across domains, from mathematical operations to relational inferences, and explains why model behavior remains brittle even under idealized prompting. We argue that LLMs function as powerful pattern completion engines, but lack the architectural scaffolding for principled, compositional reasoning. Our findings delineate the boundary of current LLM capabilities and motivate future models with metacognitive control, principle lifting, and structurally grounded execution. This diagnosis also clarifies why mechanistic interpretability findings may reflect training-specific pattern coordination rather than universal computational principles, and why the geometric separation between instruction and execution pathways suggests limitations in neural introspection and mechanistic analysis.

</details>


### [111] [Efficient Story Point Estimation With Comparative Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.14642)
*Monoshiz Mahbub Khan,Xiaoyin Xi,Andrew Meneely,Zhe Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于比较学习的框架，用于优化敏捷软件开发中的故事点估算。与传统的为每个条目分配故事点值不同，该方法要求开发人员比较条目对，并判断哪个需要更多的工作量。这种方法通过减少认知负担，可以更有效地训练机器学习模型，其预测性能与基于真实值回归的模型相当，甚至更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统敏捷软件开发中的故事点估算（如规划扑克）虽然有助于项目初期校准，但随着项目进行会变得繁琐且耗时。现有的机器学习模型（如GPT2SP和FastText-SVM）虽然能提高效率，但需要大量同一项目历史数据进行训练，缺乏跨项目或在数据量不足时的泛化能力。因此，研究旨在通过一种新的比较学习方法来简化故事点估算，降低人力成本，并提高模型在项目特定数据不足时的预测准确性。

Method: 该研究提出并评估了一种基于比较学习的框架来校准项目特定的故事点预测模型。其核心思想是，不直接要求开发人员为每个待估算的需求条目（backlog item）分配一个具体的故事点值，而是向开发人员呈现成对的需求条目，并让他们判断哪一个需要更多的估算工作量。利用这些成对的比较性判断作为训练数据，来训练一个机器学习模型进行故事点估算。研究中通过在16个项目中收集了23,313个手动估算数据来对该技术进行了实证评估，并与传统的基于回归的模型进行了比较。

Result: 研究结果表明，通过比较性判断训练出的模型，在预测值与真实故事点之间的Spearman秩相关系数平均可达0.34。这一性能与直接使用真实故事点值进行训练的回归模型相当，甚至在某些情况下更好。这证明了该比较学习方法在效率和效果上优于传统的基于回归的方法。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的比较学习方法通过要求开发人员进行相对比较而非绝对评分，显著降低了估算过程中的认知负担，符合比较判断定律。这种方法在保持或提升预测准确性的同时，提高了故事点估算的效率。未来工作可进一步探索该框架在更大规模和更多样化项目中的应用，以及与其他估算技术的融合。

Abstract: Story point estimation is an essential part of agile software development. Story points are unitless, project-specific effort estimates that help developers plan their sprints. Traditionally, developers estimate story points collaboratively using planning poker or other manual techniques. While the initial calibrating of the estimates to each project is helpful, once a team has converged on a set of precedents, story point estimation can become tedious and labor-intensive. Machine learning can reduce this burden, but only with enough context from the historical decisions made by the project team. That is, state-of-the-art models, such as GPT2SP and FastText-SVM, only make accurate predictions (within-project) when trained on data from the same project. The goal of this work is to streamline story point estimation by evaluating a comparative learning-based framework for calibrating project-specific story point prediction models. Instead of assigning a specific story point value to every backlog item, developers are presented with pairs of items, and indicate which item requires more effort. Using these comparative judgments, a machine learning model is trained to predict the story point estimates. We empirically evaluated our technique using data with 23,313 manual estimates in 16 projects. The model learned from comparative judgments can achieve on average 0.34 Spearman's rank correlation coefficient between its predictions and the ground truth story points. This is similar to, if not better than, the performance of a regression model learned from the ground truth story points. Therefore, the proposed comparative learning approach is more efficient than state-of-the-art regression-based approaches according to the law of comparative judgments - providing comparative judgments yields a lower cognitive burden on humans than providing ratings or categorical labels.

</details>


### [112] [CAMA: Enhancing Mathematical Reasoning in Large Language Models with Causal Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.02583)
*Lei Zan,Keli Zhang,Ruichu Cai,Lujia Pan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在数学推理方面存在不足，本文提出了CAMA框架，通过构建数学因果图（MCG）来显式地表示和利用数学知识的结构依赖性。CAMA分为学习和推理两个阶段：学习阶段，通过因果发现和迭代反馈构建和优化MCG；推理阶段，根据问题动态提取相关子图并引导LLM进行推理。实验结果表明，CAMA显著提升了LLM在数学问题上的表现，结构化引导优于非结构化引导，因果关系优于对称关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理复杂数学推理任务时遇到困难，这主要是由于数学知识中深层次的结构依赖性。解决这一问题对于提升LLMs的通用能力至关重要。

Method: CAMA是一个两阶段的因果框架。在学习阶段，首先通过结合LLM的先验知识和因果发现算法，从问答对语料库中构建数学因果图（MCG），该图表示解题策略及其因果依赖。然后，通过迭代反馈进一步优化MCG。在推理阶段，针对新问题，根据问题内容和LLM的中间推理过程，从MCG中动态提取相关子图，并将其注入LLM以指导其推理。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验表明，CAMA显著提高了LLM在复杂数学问题上的性能。结构化引导的性能优于非结构化引导，而考虑非对称因果关系比仅使用对称关联能带来更大的性能提升。

Conclusion: CAMA框架通过显式地引入数学知识的结构和因果关系，成功解决了大型语言模型在复杂数学推理方面的挑战。该方法不仅提升了模型的性能，而且证明了结构化和因果化引导的有效性，为未来研究如何增强LLMs的推理能力提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across a wide range of tasks, yet they still struggle with complex mathematical reasoning, a challenge fundamentally rooted in deep structural dependencies. To address this challenge, we propose \textbf{CA}usal \textbf{MA}thematician (\textbf{CAMA}), a two-stage causal framework that equips LLMs with explicit, reusable mathematical structure. In the learning stage, CAMA first constructs the \textbf{M}athematical \textbf{C}ausal \textbf{G}raph (\textbf{MCG}), a high-level representation of solution strategies, by combining LLM priors with causal discovery algorithms applied to a corpus of question-solution pairs. The resulting MCG encodes essential knowledge points and their causal dependencies. To better align the graph with downstream reasoning tasks, CAMA further refines the MCG through iterative feedback derived from a selected subset of the question-solution pairs. In the reasoning stage, given a new question, CAMA dynamically extracts a task-relevant subgraph from the MCG, conditioned on both the question content and the LLM's intermediate reasoning trace. This subgraph, which encodes the most pertinent knowledge points and their causal dependencies, is then injected back into the LLM to guide its reasoning process. Empirical results on real-world datasets show that CAMA significantly improves LLM performance on challenging mathematical problems. Furthermore, our experiments demonstrate that structured guidance consistently outperforms unstructured alternatives, and that incorporating asymmetric causal relationships yields greater improvements than using symmetric associations alone.

</details>


### [113] [Clutch Control: An Attention-based Combinatorial Bandit for Efficient Mutation in JavaScript Engine Fuzzing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.12732)
*Myles Foley,Sergio Maffeis,Muhammad Fakhrur Rozi,Takeshi Takahashi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: JavaScript引擎因其广泛应用而成为安全关注的焦点。现有模糊测试技术在选择变异目标时存在不足，通常采用随机选择。本文提出CLUTCH，一种基于深度组合赌博机的新型模糊测试方法，利用注意力机制处理可变长度的JavaScript代码表示，并通过具体Dropout动态调整探索策略。实验证明，CLUTCH在提高有效测试用例数量和覆盖率方面优于现有方法，并在波动和组合设置中显著减少了遗憾值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JavaScript引擎在Web浏览器、PDF阅读器和服务器端应用中的广泛使用，引起了对其安全性的高度关注。针对JavaScript引擎的模糊测试技术是保障其安全性的关键。然而，当前主流的模糊测试方法在选择代码变异目标时，往往采用随机策略，缺乏针对性，可能导致效率低下。因此，寻找更优的变异目标选择策略，以提升模糊测试的效率和效果，具有重要的研究意义和实际价值。

Method: 本文提出CLUTCH，一种新颖的深度组合赌博机（deep combinatorial bandit）框架，用于优化JavaScript模糊测试中的变异目标选择。CLUTCH能够处理可变长度的JavaScript测试用例表示，并引入了深度学习中的注意力机制来捕捉代码结构信息。此外，CLUTCH采用了具体Dropout（Concrete Dropout）技术，使其能够动态地调整探索（exploration）与利用（exploitation）的平衡，以适应不断变化的模糊测试环境。在实验设置中，研究人员将CLUTCH与三种最先进的解决方案进行了对比，并评估了其在生成有效测试用例、代码覆盖率以及在波动和组合设置下的遗憾值（regret）等方面的表现。

Result: CLUTCH在JavaScript模糊测试效率方面取得了显著提升。与三种最先进的解决方案相比，CLUTCH平均分别提高了20.3%的有效测试用例数量和8.9%的覆盖率/测试用例。在波动和组合设置下，CLUTCH的表现也优于现有的赌博机算法，分别实现了至少78.1%和4.1%的遗憾值降低，证明了其在复杂和动态环境下的有效性。

Conclusion: CLUTCH通过引入深度组合赌博机和注意力机制，有效地解决了现有JavaScript模糊测试中变异目标选择的难题，显著提高了测试用例的生成效率和代码覆盖率。该方法在波动和组合设置下展现出强大的性能，为未来的模糊测试技术发展提供了新的方向。未来的工作可以进一步探索CLUTCH在其他编程语言和复杂软件系统中的应用，并研究更精细化的探索策略。

Abstract: JavaScript engines are widely used in web browsers, PDF readers, and server-side applications. The rise in concern over their security has led to the development of several targeted fuzzing techniques. However, existing approaches use random selection to determine where to perform mutations in JavaScript code. We postulate that the problem of selecting better mutation targets is suitable for combinatorial bandits with a volatile number of arms. Thus, we propose CLUTCH, a novel deep combinatorial bandit that can observe variable length JavaScript test case representations, using an attention mechanism from deep learning. Furthermore, using Concrete Dropout, CLUTCH can dynamically adapt its exploration. We show that CLUTCH increases efficiency in JavaScript fuzzing compared to three state-of-the-art solutions by increasing the number of valid test cases and coverage-per-testcase by, respectively, 20.3% and 8.9% on average. In volatile and combinatorial settings we show that CLUTCH outperforms state-of-the-art bandits, achieving at least 78.1% and 4.1% less regret in volatile and combinatorial settings, respectively.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的COUP算法配置过程虽然有很好的理论保证，但在实际性能上不如一些启发式方法。本文旨在弥补这一差距，使理论驱动的算法配置在实践中更具竞争力。

Method: 本文提出了一系列对COUP的改进，以提升其实际性能，同时保持其理论保证。通过实验验证了这些改进的有效性。此外，研究还通过一个案例研究，展示了如何探索算法选择问题的解决方案对效用函数变化的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文成功地将理论上可靠的效用算法配置在实践中变得具有竞争力，通过对COUP的改进，显著提高了其实际性能。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的效用函数和算法选择场景。

Abstract: Utilitarian algorithm configuration identifies a parameter setting for a given algorithm that maximizes a user's utility. Utility functions offer a theoretically well-grounded approach to optimizing decision-making under uncertainty and are flexible enough to capture a user's preferences over algorithm runtimes (e.g., they can describe a sharp cutoff after which a solution is no longer required, a per-hour cost for compute, or diminishing returns from algorithms that take longer to run). COUP is a recently-introduced utilitarian algorithm configuration procedure which was designed mainly to offer strong theoretical guarantees about the quality of the configuration it returns, with less attention paid to its practical performance. This paper closes that gap, bringing theoretically-grounded, utilitarian algorithm configuration to the point where it is competitive with widely used, heuristic configuration procedures that offer no performance guarantees. We present a series of improvements to COUP that improve its empirical performance without degrading its theoretical guarantees and demonstrate their benefit experimentally. Using a case study, we also illustrate ways of exploring the robustness of a given solution to the algorithm selection problem to variations in the utility function.

Abstract: We propose OutboundEval, a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) in expert-level intelligent outbound calling scenarios. Second, we develop a large-model-driven User Simulator that generates diverse, persona-rich virtual users with realistic behaviors, emotional variability, and communication styles, providing a controlled yet authentic testing environment. Third, we introduce a dynamic evaluation method that adapts to task variations, integrating automated and human-in-the-loop assessment to measure task execution accuracy, professional knowledge application, adaptability, and user experience quality. Experiments on 12 state-of-the-art LLMs reveal distinct trade-offs between expert-level task completion and interaction fluency, offering practical insights for building reliable, human-like outbound AI systems. OutboundEval establishes a practical, extensible, and domain-oriented standard for benchmarking LLMs in professional applications.

### [116] [Large Language Model-assisted Autonomous Vehicle Recovery from Immobilization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26023)
*Zhipeng Bao,Qianwen Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为StuckSolver的新型大语言模型（LLM）驱动的自动驾驶汽车（AV）恢复框架，旨在解决AV在特定交通场景下（例如，需要人类驾驶员擅长处理的场景）的“动弹不得”问题，这些问题会导致交通堵塞。与需要昂贵远程干预或限制可访问性的手动接管方案不同，StuckSolver作为一个即插即用模块，能够通过自我推理和/或乘客指导来解决这些僵局。它通过标准传感器数据流与AV的现有感知-规划-控制堆栈接口，无需修改AV内部架构。评估结果表明，StuckSolver在Bench2Drive基准和自定义不确定性场景中，仅凭自主推理就能达到接近最先进的性能，并且在结合乘客指导后性能有所提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自动驾驶汽车（AV）在近几十年取得了显著进展，但在某些人类驾驶员擅长应对的交通场景中，AV仍然面临挑战，常常会动弹不得，从而扰乱整体交通流量。现有的恢复解决方案，例如远程干预（成本高且效率低）和手动接管（排除不具备驾驶能力的乘客，并限制了AV的可访问性），都存在不足。因此，迫切需要一种更有效、更易于访问的AV恢复机制，以应对这些复杂情况，确保交通流畅性和AV的广泛应用。

Method: 本研究引入了一个名为StuckSolver的新型框架，该框架利用大型语言模型（LLM）来解决AV在动弹不得的场景。StuckSolver被设计为一个即插即用附加模块，可在AV现有的感知-规划-控制堆栈之上运行，无需修改AV的内部架构。它通过标准的传感器数据流进行接口操作，以检测动弹不得的状态，解读环境背景，并生成可由AV的本地规划器执行的高级恢复命令。该框架支持两种模式：1）自主自我推理，AV自行解决；2）乘客指导，AV与乘客协作解决。实验在Bench2Drive基准和自定义设计的不确定性场景中进行评估。

Result: 在Bench2Drive基准和自定义设计的不确定性场景的评估中，StuckSolver展示了其有效性。结果表明，仅通过自主自我推理，StuckSolver就能达到接近最先进的性能水平。更重要的是，当结合乘客指导时，StuckSolver的性能得到了进一步提升，证明了人机协作在解决复杂自动驾驶场景中的潜力。

Conclusion: StuckSolver作为一个基于LLM的恢复框架，成功地解决了自动驾驶汽车在动弹不得场景下的挑战，提高了交通的流畅性和AV的可访问性。该方法通过自我推理和乘客指导，在评估中取得了令人鼓舞的结果，并达到了接近最先进的性能。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的场景，优化LLM的推理能力，并研究更精细的人机交互界面。

Abstract: Despite significant advancements in recent decades, autonomous vehicles (AVs) continue to face challenges in navigating certain traffic scenarios where human drivers excel. In such situations, AVs often become immobilized, disrupting overall traffic flow. Current recovery solutions, such as remote intervention (which is costly and inefficient) and manual takeover (which excludes non-drivers and limits AV accessibility), are inadequate. This paper introduces StuckSolver, a novel Large Language Model (LLM) driven recovery framework that enables AVs to resolve immobilization scenarios through self-reasoning and/or passenger-guided decision-making. StuckSolver is designed as a plug-in add-on module that operates on top of the AV's existing perception-planning-control stack, requiring no modification to its internal architecture. Instead, it interfaces with standard sensor data streams to detect immobilization states, interpret environmental context, and generate high-level recovery commands that can be executed by the AV's native planner. We evaluate StuckSolver on the Bench2Drive benchmark and in custom-designed uncertainty scenarios. Results show that StuckSolver achieves near-state-of-the-art performance through autonomous self-reasoning alone and exhibits further improvements when passenger guidance is incorporated.

### [117] [Synthetic Data-Driven Prompt Tuning for Financial QA over Tables and Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.06292)
*Yaoning Yu,Kai-Min Chang,Ye Yu,Kai Wei,Haojing Luo,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“数据增强优化驱动的自改进提示框架”的新方法，用于提高大型语言模型在处理金融文档（如财报和资产负债表）时的数字推理能力。与依赖固定数据集或手动标注的方法不同，该框架通过生成合成的金融表格和文档片段，验证其正确性和鲁棒性，并据此优化提示，形成一个闭环的自学习过程。实验结果表明，该方法在DocMath-Eval基准测试中，在准确性和鲁棒性方面均优于标准的提示方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融文档（如财报、资产负债表）通常包含大量表格和多页报告，理解和进行数字推理具有挑战性。大型语言模型（LLMs）在这一领域展现出潜力，但其表现严重依赖于提示（prompt）的质量。现有方法主要依赖于在固定数据集上微调提示，这限制了模型适应新问题类型或文档结构的能力，或者需要成本高昂且耗费人力的数据标注。因此，研究需要一种能够自适应、无需外部标注即可提升LLMs在金融领域数字推理能力的提示优化方法。

Method: 本研究提出的框架是一个数据增强优化驱动的自改进提示系统。它包含三个核心组件：1. **合成数据生成器**：生成新的、可能暴露当前提示弱点的合成金融表格和文档片段。2. **验证器**：检查生成示例的正确性（accuracy）和鲁棒性（robustness）。3. **提示优化器**：根据验证结果，逐步优化提示。整个过程形成一个闭环反馈循环：生成器创造新样本，验证器评估样本，优化器依据评估结果调整提示，然后重复此过程。这种迭代反馈机制使得提示能够持续改进，而无需外部人工标注的数据。

Result: 在DocMath-Eval基准测试上的评估结果显示，该研究提出的自改进提示框架在金融数字推理任务上，相比于标准的提示方法，在准确性和鲁棒性两方面均取得了更高的性能。这证明了该方法在提升LLMs处理复杂金融数据方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种创新的自改进提示框架，通过数据增强优化，显著提升了大型语言模型在金融文档数字推理任务上的表现，尤其是在准确性和鲁棒性方面。该方法避免了对昂贵手动标注数据的依赖，为金融领域的LLM应用提供了一种更高效、更具适应性的解决方案。未来的工作可以探索将此框架应用于更广泛的金融任务，以及进一步提升合成数据生成和验证的效率和多样性。

Abstract: Financial documents like earning reports or balance sheets often involve long tables and multi-page reports. Large language models have become a new tool to help numerical reasoning and understanding these documents. However, prompt quality can have a major effect on how well LLMs perform these financial reasoning tasks. Most current methods tune prompts on fixed datasets of financial text or tabular data, which limits their ability to adapt to new question types or document structures, or they involve costly and manually labeled/curated dataset to help build the prompts. We introduce a self-improving prompt framework driven by data-augmented optimization. In this closed-loop process, we generate synthetic financial tables and document excerpts, verify their correctness and robustness, and then update the prompt based on the results. Specifically, our framework combines a synthetic data generator with verifiers and a prompt optimizer, where the generator produces new examples that exposes weaknesses in the current prompt, the verifiers check the validity and robustness of the produced examples, and the optimizer incrementally refines the prompt in response. By iterating these steps in a feedback cycle, our method steadily improves prompt accuracy on financial reasoning tasks without needing external labels. Evaluation on DocMath-Eval benchmark demonstrates that our system achieves higher performance in both accuracy and robustness than standard prompt methods, underscoring the value of incorporating synthetic data generation into prompt learning for financial applications.

### [118] [Data Complexity of Querying Description Logic Knowledge Bases under Cost-Based Semantics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.07095)
*Meghyn Bienvenu,Quentin Manière*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究深入探讨了在引入成本计算语义后，查询不一致的加权描述逻辑（DL）知识库的数据复杂度问题。研究重点在于分析具有逆关系和关系包含的DL（涵盖了DL-Lite的主要方言），并显著超越了现有的数据复杂度结果，包括提升了若干下界，并确定了最优成本确定性答案语义的精确复杂度。尤其值得注意的是，研究发现对于DL-LiteHbool本体和固定成本界限，实例查询的确定性答案以及连接查询的可能答案可以通过一阶重写来计算，数据复杂度达到了最低的TC0级别，这与以往研究普遍显示的成本计算语义的不可处理性形成了鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的描述逻辑（DL）知识库在处理不一致信息时存在困难，而现实世界中的知识库往往包含不一致性。成本计算语义的引入为解决这一问题提供了新的视角，它通过为违反公理和断言的解释分配成本，来定义查询的确定性答案和可能答案。然而，先前对成本计算语义的研究主要集中在较简单的DLs（如EL⊥到ALCO），并未充分涵盖更复杂的包含逆关系和关系包含的DLs（如DL-Lite方言）。因此，有必要深入研究这些更复杂DLs在成本计算语义下的数据复杂度，并探索是否存在比普遍认为的更优的计算可能性。

Method: 本研究采用数据复杂度分析方法，研究了在引入成本计算语义的加权描述逻辑（DL）知识库中的查询问题。研究扩展了对DLs的分析范围，使其包含逆关系和关系包含，从而覆盖了DL-Lite的主要方言。通过精确分析最优成本确定性答案语义的复杂度，并锐化了若干下界，研究显著扩展了现有结果。核心方法是利用一阶重写技术，在特定条件下（DL-LiteHbool本体和固定成本界限）实现了对实例查询的确定性答案和连接查询的可能答案的有效计算。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于包含逆关系和关系包含的DLs，在成本计算语义下，查询复杂度的分析有了显著进展。研究锐化了若干下界，并首次确定了最优成本确定性答案语义的确切数据复杂度。最重要且出人意料的发现是，在DL-LiteHbool本体和固定成本界限的条件下，实例查询的确定性答案和连接查询的可能答案可以通过一阶重写来计算，数据复杂度达到了最低的TC0级别。这表明在特定条件下，原本被认为普遍存在的不可处理性是可以克服的。

Conclusion: 本研究在成本计算语义和数据复杂度分析领域取得了重要进展。通过将分析扩展到包含逆关系和关系包含的DLs，并提出了基于一阶重写的高效计算方法，研究不仅深化了对复杂DLs不一致信息处理的理解，而且在特定情况下克服了普遍存在的计算障碍。研究结果表明，在DL-LiteHbool本体和固定成本界限下，查询复杂性可以达到TC0级别，这对于实际应用具有重要意义。未来的工作可以进一步探索其他DLs的成本计算语义，以及更广泛的查询类型和成本计算模型。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the data complexity of querying inconsistent weighted description logic (DL) knowledge bases under recently-introduced cost-based semantics. In a nutshell, the idea is to assign each interpretation a cost based upon the weights of the violated axioms and assertions, and certain and possible query answers are determined by considering all (resp. some) interpretations having optimal or bounded cost. Whereas the initial study of cost-based semantics focused on DLs between $\mathcal{EL}_\bot$ and $\mathcal{ALCO}$, we consider DLs that may contain inverse roles and role inclusions, thus covering prominent DL-Lite dialects. Our data complexity analysis goes significantly beyond existing results by sharpening several lower bounds and pinpointing the precise complexity of optimal-cost certain answer semantics (no non-trivial upper bound was known). Moreover, while all existing results show the intractability of cost-based semantics, our most challenging and surprising result establishes that if we consider $\text{DL-Lite}^\mathcal{H}_\mathsf{bool}$ ontologies and a fixed cost bound, certain answers for instance queries and possible answers for conjunctive queries can be computed using first-order rewriting and thus enjoy the lowest possible data complexity ($\mathsf{TC}_0$).

</details>

### [119] [Decomposition of Methane Diluted with Inert Gas in an RF Discharge Cell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10937)
*Sophia Gershman,Mikhail N. Shneider,Yevgeny Raitses*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了射频电容耦合放电模式对甲烷分解及其产物选择性的影响，发现在Ar和Kr中，放电模式会从均匀过渡到条纹状，或从弥散过渡到收缩，而在He和Ne中则保持均匀和弥散。研究结果表明，收缩放电模式在含5%或更少CH4的Ar/CH4和Kr/CH4混合物中能实现高达99.7%的甲烷分解率，并生成乙炔和石墨化固体碳等有价值产物。这揭示了放电模式，特别是收缩模式，在高效甲烷分解和制备增值产品中的关键作用，并指出电子和热性质均对此效应负责。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 甲烷分解制氢和碳纳米材料具有重要意义，但等离子体放电模式对甲烷分解的影响机制尚不明确，阻碍了等离子体辅助化学转化的优化。因此，研究放电模式与产物选择性的耦合关系，以期找到高效分解甲烷的放电条件，具有重要研究价值和应用前景。

Method: 本研究在2-3 torr的压力范围内，使用射频电容耦合放电装置，研究了甲烷/惰性气体混合物中的放电行为。通过改变惰性气体（Ar, Kr, He, Ne）和甲烷的比例，观察放电模式（均匀、条纹状、弥散、收缩）的变化。同时，建立了Ar/CH4放电的0-D模型，分析了Ar亚稳态粒子在解离和电离过程中的作用。通过测量甲烷分解率和产物（乙炔、石墨化固体碳等）的生成情况，评估不同放电模式的效果。

Result: 在Ar和Kr中，随着甲烷比例的增加（5%或更少），放电模式从均匀过渡到条纹状，或从弥散过渡到收缩。He和Ne的放电模式始终保持均匀和弥散。0-D模型指出，Ar亚稳态粒子在解离和电离过程中至关重要，并确定了放电收缩的阈值。在含5%或更少CH4的Ar/CH4和Kr/CH4混合物中，收缩放电模式实现了高达99.7%的甲烷分解率，主要产物为乙炔和石墨化固体碳。电子和热性质共同导致了放电收缩对甲烷分解的促进作用。

Conclusion: 放电模式，特别是收缩放电模式，在含5%或更少CH4的Ar/CH4和Kr/CH4混合物中，对实现高效率的甲烷分解（高达99.7%）和制备有价值的碳纳米材料（如石墨化固体碳）起着关键作用。放电的收缩现象受气体电子和热性质的共同影响。未来的研究可以进一步探索不同气体组分和操作条件下放电模式的调控，以及收缩放电模式在其他等离子体化学反应中的应用。

Abstract: Decomposition of methane using non-thermal plasmas is an attractive route for producing hydrogen-rich gases and valuable carbon nanomaterials. Understanding how plasma discharge modes influence methane decomposition in optimizing plasma-assisted chemical conversion remains unexplored. This study explores the coupling between the discharge structure and product selectivity in RF capacitively coupled discharges operating in methane/inert gas mixtures in the pressure range of 2 to 3 torr. The discharge exhibits mode transitions from uniform to striated in Ar and Kr and from diffuse to contracted in Ar and Kr with 5 percent or less CH4. The discharges in He and Ne remained uniform under our operating conditions, and their mixtures with CH4 remained diffuse. A 0-D model for Ar/CH4 discharge established a threshold for contraction while also asserting the importance of Ar metastable in the dissociation and ionization processes. The highest degree of methane decomposition, 99.7% with the main products of acetylene and graphitized solid carbon was achieved in the contracted discharge mode for both Kr or Ar with 5% or less CH4. We demonstrate that contraction can play a crucial role in the effective decomposition of methane with value-added products and that both the electronic and thermal properties of plasma gas are responsible for this effect.

</details>


### [120] [Studies of laser stimulated photodetachment from nanoparticles for particle charge measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10956)
*Y. A. Ussenov,M. N. Shneider,S. Yatom,Y. Raitses*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 由于纳米颗粒的生长、等离子体性质的变化以及难以观察单个颗粒，传统的微粒荷电诊断方法在尘埃等离子体中无效。本研究采用激光激发的光解吸附（LSPD）技术测量纳米颗粒的平均电荷。通过在氩气和乙炔混合物中使用电容耦合射频放电生长纳米颗粒，并利用朗缪尔探针监测LSPD引起的电子电流变化。结果表明，在不同生长阶段，电子电流脉冲的衰减时间较长，这归因于残留的负离子的存在。通过激光消光法测得的颗粒密度，估算出平均直径约为154.3 nm的颗粒的电荷约为16个基本电荷单位。该值低于轨道运动限制（OML）理论的预测，这在纳米尘埃等离子体中是常见的，因为电子会大量耗尽。研究证实了LSPD方法在测量纳米颗粒电荷方面的适用性，但也强调了背景负离子对脱附电流衰减的影响，需要仔细考虑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与微粒相比，由于生长引起的尺寸变化、等离子体性质的显著变化以及观察单个颗粒的困难，确定纳米颗粒的电荷更具挑战性，这使得传统的微粒电荷诊断方法在尘埃等离子体中无效。因此，需要一种新的方法来准确测量纳米颗粒的电荷。

Method: 本研究采用激光激发的光解吸附（LSPD）技术来测定纳米颗粒的平均电荷。通过在氩气和乙炔混合物中使用电容耦合射频放电来生长纳米颗粒。利用圆柱形朗缪尔探针监测LSPD引起的电子电流变化。在不同的粉尘生长阶段收集并分析LSPD信号。利用激光消光法测量的颗粒密度来估算每粒子电荷。

Result: 研究发现，电子电流脉冲的延长衰减可归因于残留负离子的存在，这些离子被有效静电捕获，并在LSPD后重新形成。对于平均直径Dp约为154.3 nm的颗粒，估算的电荷Qd约为16个基本电荷单位。测得的电荷值低于轨道运动限制（OML）理论的预测值，这在纳米尘埃等离子体中是常见现象，原因是电子大量耗尽。

Conclusion: LSPD在氩气和乙炔纳米尘埃等离子体中测量单个纳米颗粒电荷的结果证实了该方法的适用性。然而，研究也强调，背景负离子的电子脱附会影响脱附电流的衰减，并且在分析结果时必须仔细考虑这一点。未来的研究可以进一步探索优化LSPD参数以减少背景负离子的影响，并将其应用于更广泛的纳米尘埃等离子体系统。

Abstract: Determining nanoparticle charge is more challenging than that for microparticles due to growth-induced size changes, substantial plasma property variations, and difficulties in visualizing individual particles, rendering conventional microparticle charge diagnostics ineffective in dusty plasma. In this work, we utilized laser-stimulated photodetachment (LSPD) to deduce the mean charge of nanoparticles. Nanoparticles were grown in an Ara and C2H2 mixture using a capacitively coupled RF discharge and the LSPD induced changes in the electron current monitored by a cylindrical Langmuir probe. LSPD signals were obtained and analyzed across different dust growth phases. The prolonged decay of electron current pulses was attributed to the presence of residual negative ions, caused by the effective electrostatic trapping of these ions and the potential post - LSPD re-formation of new ones. The charge per particle was estimated using known values of particle density obtained by laser-light extinction method. For particles with mean diameter Dp ~ 154.3 nm, the charge found to be of Qd~16 elementary charge units. The charge values appear to be lower than the values predicted by orbital motion limited (OML) theory. This deviation is commonly observed in nanodusty plasmas due to significant electron depletion. LSPD results in Ar and C2H2 nano-dusty plasma confirm the applicability of these method for estimating individual nanoparticle charges. However, it has also been demonstrated that electron detachment from residual background negative ions can influence the detachment current decay and must be carefully considered

</details>


### [121] [Investigation of Stimulated Brillouin Scattering Driven by Broadband Lasers in High-Z Plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.11395)
*Xiaoran Li,Jie Qiu,Liang Hao,Shiyang Zou*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 在高Z等离子体中，使用一维碰撞粒子- in -细胞模拟研究了宽带激光驱动的受激布里渊散射（SBS）。研究发现，宽带激光的相干时间缩短会削弱三波耦合，并持续降低SBS的时间增长率，但饱和反射率在带宽超过临界阈值之前基本保持不变。只有当激光带宽超过SBS时间增长率的几十倍时，才能有效抑制SBS。AuB等离子体相比Au等离子体，SBS增长率和反射率有所降低，且在较低带宽下即可抑制SBS。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受激布里渊散射（SBS）在激光-等离子体相互作用中是一个关键问题，尤其是在惯性约束聚变（ICF）等应用中。宽带激光被认为是抑制SBS的有效手段，但其在高Z等离子体中的演化机制和有效抑制条件尚不完全清楚。本研究旨在深入理解宽带激光在高Z等离子体中驱动SBS的机制，并确定有效的抑制条件。

Method: 本研究利用一维碰撞粒子- in -细胞（PIC）模拟来研究高Z等离子体中由宽带激光驱动的SBS。通过改变激光强度和带宽等参数，模拟了SBS的演化过程，并分析了激光相干时间、三波耦合、增长率和饱和反射率等关键指标。此外，还对比了Au和AuB等离子体中的模拟结果，以评估等离子体成分对SBS抑制的影响。

Result: 模拟结果表明，宽带激光的相干时间缩短会削弱三波耦合，并持续降低SBS的时间增长率。然而，饱和反射率在激光带宽超过某个临界阈值之前几乎保持不变。只有当激光带宽显著超过SBS的时间增长率（约几十倍）时，才能实现有效的SBS抑制。在AuB等离子体中，SBS的增长率和反射率均低于Au等离子体，且抑制现象在较低带宽下即可出现，表明等离子体成分对SBS抑制效果有影响。

Conclusion: 本研究通过一维PIC模拟，揭示了宽带激光在高Z等离子体中抑制SBS的详细机制。研究强调了激光带宽与激光强度之间的耦合依赖性，并提出了有效的抑制条件：激光带宽需远大于SBS的时间增长率。此外，等离子体成分（如AuB）也会影响SBS的抑制效果。这些发现对于优化宽带激光设计以实现惯性约束聚变中的SBS有效控制具有重要的指导意义。

Abstract: The evolution of stimulated Brillouin scattering (SBS) driven by broadband lasers in high-Z plasmas is investigated using one-dimensional collisional particle-in-cell simulations. The temporal incoherence of broadband lasers modulates the pump intensity, generating stochastic intensity pulses that intermittently drive SBS. The shortened coherence time weakens the three-wave coupling and continuously reduces the temporal growth rate, while the saturated reflectivity remains nearly unchanged until the bandwidth exceeds a critical threshold. Simulations with varying laser intensities and bandwidths reveal a consistent scaling behavior, indicating that effective suppression occurs only when the laser bandwidth exceeds the temporal growth rate of SBS by several tens of times. Comparative simulations in Au and AuB plasmas exhibit similar suppression trends, with AuB showing reduced SBS growth rate and reflectivity, and the onset of suppression occurring at a lower bandwidth. These findings elucidate the coupled dependence of SBS mitigation on bandwidth and laser intensity in high-Z plasmas, offering useful guidance for optimizing broadband laser designs in inertial confinement fusion.

</details>


### [122] [Coherent synchrotron radiation by excitation of surface plasmon polariton on near-critical solid microtube surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.04561)
*Bifeng Lei,Hao Zhang,Daniel Seipt,Alexandre Bonatto,Bin Qiao,Javier Resta-Lopez,Guoxing Xia,Carsten Welsch*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种利用表面等离激元激发的相干同步辐射（CSR）新机制，可在微管内产生类超辐射的X射线，相干性可提升高达两个数量级，为开发强大的超短光源提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发强大的超短光源对于材料科学、生物成像等领域至关重要。现有的相干同步辐射（CSR）技术在产生高相干性光源方面仍有提升空间，特别是对于超短脉冲光源。本研究旨在探索一种新的CSR产生机制，以克服现有技术的局限性，实现更高相干性的X射线发射。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于表面等离激元极化激元（SPPs）的广义超辐射CSR产生机制。具体方法包括：1. 利用固体、近临界密度微管内表面上共振激发的SPPs。2. 通过沿微管轴线传播的高强度圆偏振激光脉冲，有效地耦合圆柱形SPPs模式，形成方位角结构化的旋转电磁场。3. 旋转电磁场约束、调制并直接加速表面电子，使其在Vavilov-Cherenkov角发射CSR。4. 通过提高电子的方位角对称性，实现各项方位角方向上的孤立谐波CSR发射，即使在相干性不完全的情况下也能显著增强辐射强度。5. 使用全3D粒子- in-Cell（PIC）模拟来验证该方案的可行性，并评估产生的X射线的相干性增强效果。

Result: 研究结果表明，该方法能够通过激发SPPs产生CSR，并实现类超辐射发射。全3D PIC模拟显示，与非相干发射相比，该方案产生的X射线相干性可增强高达两个数量级。通过优化电子的螺旋调制，可以实现跨所有方位角方向的孤立谐波CSR发射，从而显著提高辐射强度。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种新颖的、基于表面等离激元激发的广义超辐射CSR机制，有望在微管内产生高相干性的X射线，为开发强大的超短光源提供了有前景的解决方案。尽管实验实现面临一些挑战，例如需要高对比度激光和高精度的微管制造与对准，但这些挑战在现有或近期可及的实验能力范围内。未来的工作可以集中在克服这些实验挑战，并进一步优化该方案以实现更优越的光源性能。

Abstract: Coherent synchrotron radiation (CSR) is crucial for the development of powerful ultrashort light sources. We present a mechanism for generating CSR in the form of generalised superradiance, based on surface plasmon polaritons (SPPs), which are resonantly excited on a solid, near-critical-density inner surface of a microtube. A high-intensity, circularly polarised laser pulse, propagating along the microtube axis, efficiently couples the cylindrical SPP modes. This process creates azimuthally structured, rotating electromagnetic fields. These rotating fields subsequently confine, modulate, and directly accelerate surface electrons to emit CSR in the Vavilov-Cherenkov angle. We further demonstrate that by improving the azimuthal symmetry of these electrons, the helical modulation enables CSR emission across all azimuthal directions in the form of isolated harmonics, significantly enhancing radiation intensity even when full coherence is imperfect. Our full 3D Particle-in-Cell simulations indicate this scheme can generate X-rays with coherence enhanced by up to two orders of magnitude compared to incoherent emission. The challenges to experimentally realise this scheme are discussed, including the need for high-contrast lasers to prevent pre-plasma formation and the demanding tolerances for microtube fabrication and alignment, while these challenges are not beyond the scope of existing or near-future experimental capabilities.

</details>


### [123] [Multi-Machine Scaling Laws for Fuel and Impurity Puffing Rates Sufficient for Detachment Access: a Systematic Review of Magnetic Confinement Fusion Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.20523)
*M. Moscheni,A. Herrmann,R. Kembleton,M. Kryjak,S. Lazerson,F. Levi,M. Siccinio,P. Staniec,T. Giegerich,C. Tantos,the Gauss Fusion GmbH Team*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含457个实验和数值条目的数据库，涵盖32种不同的聚变装置（包括托卡马克、仿星器和线性等离子体装置）。基于该数据库，研究人员推导出了多装置的放电预测定律，能够预测为实现等离子体边缘分离（等离子体-墙相互作用的关键解决方案）所需的燃料和杂质注入速率。研究结果表明， শুধুমাত্র  the divertor volume, and plasma opacity are strongly correlated with fuelling rates. The derived scaling laws, such as $Γ_{	ext{D}} o [n_{	ext{sep}} a (S_{	ext{div}}/V_{	ext{div}})^{-1.5}]^{1.05}$ for toroidal devices and $Γ_{	ext{D}}^{	ext{HDL}} o 0.43 a^{1.58} λ_q^{-0.89}$ for H-mode plasmas, demonstrate good agreement with experimental data. A general nonlinear law is also established for impurity seeding rates, yielding the simplification $Γ_{	ext{Z}}^{	ext{GES}} o a^{1.51} λ_q^{-0.27}$. These findings have immediate implications for reactor design and edge plasma modeling, offering physics-based 0D laws to connect detachment access with engineering actuators.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离子体-墙相互作用是聚变反应堆设计中的一个重大挑战。等离子体边缘分离是解决这一挑战的最有前景的方案，然而，实现和控制分离所需的燃料和杂质注入速率尚不清楚，尤其是在不同类型的聚变装置之间。因此，需要建立能够跨装置预测这些注入速率的标度律，以指导反应堆的设计和运行。

Method: 研究人员首先收集并整合了一个包含457个实验和数值条目的数据库，这些条目涵盖了32种不同的聚变装置（包括托卡马克、仿星器和线性等离子体装置）。然后，他们利用该数据集推导出了多装置的放电预测定律，这些定律能够预测实现等离子体边缘分离所需的燃料和杂质注入速率。研究中考虑了多种因素，如分离器体积、等离子体不透明度、密度、装置尺寸以及功率下降长度等。所得标度律经过了与40个L模和H模等离子体实验数据的验证，评估了其预测精度。

Result: 研究推导出了适用于不同聚变装置的燃料和杂质注入速率标度律。对于所有环形装置，燃料注入速率的标度律为 $Γ_{	ext{D}} o [n_{	ext{sep}} a (S_{	ext{div}}/V_{	ext{div}})^{-1.5}]^{1.05}$，其中 $n_{	ext{sep}}$ 是分离器边缘密度，$a$ 是装置半径，$S_{	ext{div}}$ 是分离器表面积，$V_{	ext{div}}$ 是分离器体积。对于H模等离子体，提出了简化的标度律 $Γ_{	ext{D}}^{	ext{HDL}} o 0.43 a^{1.58} λ_q^{-0.89}$，其中 $λ_q$ 是功率下降长度，该公式不直接依赖于 $n_{	ext{sep}}$。杂质注入速率则由一个通用的非线性定律描述，并得到了简化形式 $Γ_{	ext{Z}}^{	ext{GES}} o a^{1.51} λ_q^{-0.27}$。这些标度律在与实验数据的对比中显示出良好的一致性，平均误差在2倍以内，约50%的情况下误差在一个半因子内。研究还发现，分离器体积是影响燃料注入速率的关键因素。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个跨装置的等离子体边缘分离数据库，并从中推导出了预测燃料和杂质注入速率的标度律。这些基于物理的0D标度律能够可靠地将分离的实现与工程参数联系起来，为聚变反应堆的设计和边缘等离子体建模提供了实用的工具。研究结果强调了标度律在宏观层面捕捉跨装置共性的能力，并为未来深入研究机组特定行为奠定了基础。尽管仿星器的标度律仍需进一步验证，但本研究无疑为聚变能源的实际应用迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: An open-source database of 457 experimental and numerical entries representing 32 machines$-$including tokamaks, stellarators, and linear plasma devices$-$is assembled. From this dataset, we derive multi-machine scaling laws that predict the fuel and impurity puffing rates sufficient to edge plasma detachment$-$the leading reactor-relevant solution to the challenge of plasma-wall interaction. Validation against up to 40 L- and H-mode plasmas shows agreement within a factor of 1.5 in about 50\% of cases, and within a factor of 2 on average. Divertor volume alone is found to strongly correlate with the fuelling rate. Inclusion of plasma opaqueness leads to $Γ_{\text{D}} \propto [n_{\text{sep}}\, a\, (S_{\text{div}}/V_{\text{div}})^{-1.5}]^{1.05}$, valid across all toroidal devices. Its H-mode simplification, $Γ_{\text{D}}^{\text{HDL}} \propto 0.43\, a^{1.58}\, λ_q^{-0.89}$, avoids explicit dependence on $n_{\text{sep}}$ and carries intrinsic physical meaning through the H/L density limit and the power fall-off length. The impurity seeding rate is captured by a general non-linear law, from which the Greenwald-Eich-Scarabosio simplification, $Γ_{\text{Z}}^{\text{GES}} \propto a^{1.51}\, λ_q^{-0.27}$, is obtained. Similar relationships are defined for stellarators, consistent with tokamak trends but still awaiting validation$-$an opportunity for further study. These results have immediate relevance for reactor fuel-cycle design and edge plasma modelling. More broadly, they demonstrate that physics-based 0D laws can reliably link detachment access to engineering actuators, offering practical tools for reactor design. Our laws represent macroscopic patterns across machines rather than microscopic variations within an individual device$-$providing the basis for our forthcoming studies aimed at extending this framework to machine-specific behaviour.

</details>


<div id='cs.MA'></div>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [124] [Who Gets the Reward, Who Gets the Blame? Evaluation-Aligned Training Signals for Multi-LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10687)
*Chih-Hsuan Yang,Tanwi Mallick,Le Chen,Krishnan Raghavan,Azton Wells,Amal Gueroudji,Ian T. Foster,Rajeev Thakur*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将系统级评估转化为智能体和消息级学习信号的理论框架，结合了合作博弈论归因和过程奖励建模，以解决大型语言模型（LLM）在多智能体系统（MAS）中训练方法与系统评估脱节的问题。该框架生成局部、有符号且信贷守恒的信号，用于指导MAS的训练，在成功案例中公平分配结果并促进合作，在失败案例中定位错误并奖励纠正行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLM）在多智能体系统（MAS）中的训练方法，在将系统级评估与智能体级和消息级学习联系起来方面缺乏原则性的方法。这导致了在复杂任务中，智能体难以学习到如何有效地进行协作，并且难以将系统的整体表现归因于各个智能体或消息的贡献。研究的意义在于，开发一种能够将全局系统评估转化为局部学习信号的机制，从而改进MAS的训练效率和性能。

Method: 本文提出了一种理论框架，该框架融合了合作博弈论中的归因方法（如Shapley值）和过程奖励建模（PRM）。具体来说，该框架首先利用合作博弈论的方法将系统级评估（例如任务成功或失败）分配给各个智能体（智能体级信用分配）。然后，通过过程奖励建模，将智能体级的信用进一步分解为针对每个消息（或交互步骤）的奖励信号。在成功的情况下，Shapley值被用来公平地分配结果，并转化为促进合作、抑制冗余或破坏行为的每条消息的奖励。在失败的情况下，该方法能够进行“首次错误定位”，识别导致失败的关键步骤，并生成能够惩罚有害行为但奖励纠正尝试的信号。该框架生成的信号是局部、有符号、信贷守恒的，并且与基于强化学习或偏好排序的训练方法兼容。

Result: 由于本文的贡献在于理论框架的提出，并未进行实际的实验验证，因此没有具体的实验结果。作者表明，其提出的理论框架生成了“局部、有符号、信贷守恒的信号”，并且“与基于强化学习或偏好排序的训练方法兼容”。该框架旨在提供一个“统一且可审计的路径，从全局评估到LLM多智能体训练的局部监督”。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种新颖的理论框架，旨在弥合大型语言模型（LLM）在多智能体系统（MAS）中训练时，系统级评估与智能体及消息级学习之间的鸿沟。通过结合合作博弈论归因和过程奖励建模，该框架能够将全局任务表现转化为局部、可操作的学习信号，从而指导智能体的行为。该框架的理论贡献在于提供了一个统一、有原则的方法来解决信用分配问题，并在成功和失败场景下生成有意义的训练信号。然而，该研究的局限性在于目前仅停留在理论层面，缺乏实证验证。未来的工作将集中在对该理论框架进行实证评估，以验证其在实际MAS任务中的有效性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) in multi-agent systems (MAS) have shown promise for complex tasks, yet current training methods lack principled ways to connect system-level evaluation with agent-level and message-level learning. We propose a theoretical framework that unifies cooperative game-theoretic attribution with process reward modeling to transform system evaluation into agent credit and then into response-level signals. Unlike prior approaches that rely only on attribution (e.g., Shapley) or step-level labels (e.g., PRM), our method produces local, signed, and credit-conserving signals. In success cases, Shapley-based credit assignment fairly allocates outcomes across agents and is refined into per-message rewards that promote cooperation while discouraging redundancy or sabotage. In failure cases, first-error localization yields repair-aware preferences that penalize harmful steps while rewarding corrective attempts. The resulting signals are bounded, cooperative, and directly compatible with reinforcement-based or preference-based post-training, providing a unified and auditable pathway from global evaluation to local supervision in LLM multi-agent training. Our contribution is conceptual: we present a theoretical foundation and training signals, leaving empirical validation for future work.

</details>


### [125] [Exposing Weak Links in Multi-Agent Systems under Adversarial Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10949)
*Nirmit Arora,Sathvik Joel,Ishan Kavathekar,Palak,Rohan Gandhi,Yash Pandya,Tanuja Ganu,Aditya Kanade,Akshay Nambi*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: LLM驱动的多智能体系统（MAS）日益普及，但现有安全研究多集中于单智能体，忽视了MAS特有的安全风险。本文提出了SafeAgents框架，用于细粒度评估MAS安全性，并引入Dharma指标诊断薄弱环节。研究发现，常见的MAS设计模式（如中心化控制、原子指令委托）存在严重漏洞，影响鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在MAS中的广泛应用，特别是向实际场景的迁移，其安全性变得至关重要。然而，当前研究主要关注单智能体安全，未能充分理解MAS设计带来的独特安全漏洞。现有系统因缺乏统一的框架和针对MAS特有拒绝模式的度量标准而存在不足。

Method: 本文提出了SafeAgents，一个统一且可扩展的框架，用于对MAS进行细粒度的安全评估。SafeAgents系统性地暴露了设计选择（如计划构建策略、智能体间上下文共享和后备行为）如何影响其对对抗性提示的敏感性。研究引入了Dharma，一个诊断度量标准，帮助识别多智能体管道中的薄弱环节。实验在五种广泛采用的多智能体架构（中心化、去中心化和混合变体）以及涵盖Web任务、工具使用和代码生成的四个数据集上进行了广泛研究。

Result: 研究发现，常见的MAS设计模式存在显著漏洞。例如，将任务仅委托给子智能体的中心化系统会隐藏有害目标，从而降低鲁棒性。在五种MAS架构和四个数据集上的全面研究表明，设计选择对安全性有重大影响。具体指标和性能比较可在原文中找到。

Conclusion: 本文的研究结果强调了在MAS设计中需要考虑安全性。SafeAgents框架和Dharma指标为评估和改进MAS安全性提供了有力工具。尽管现有设计模式存在漏洞，但通过安全意识的设计可以提高MAS的鲁棒性。未来的工作可以进一步扩展SafeAgents以涵盖更多类型的攻击和MAS架构。代码已在https://github.com/microsoft/SafeAgents 提供。

Abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly deployed in multi-agent systems (MAS). As these systems move toward real-world applications, their security becomes paramount. Existing research largely evaluates single-agent security, leaving a critical gap in understanding the vulnerabilities introduced by multi-agent design. However, existing systems fall short due to lack of unified frameworks and metrics focusing on unique rejection modes in MAS. We present SafeAgents, a unified and extensible framework for fine-grained security assessment of MAS. SafeAgents systematically exposes how design choices such as plan construction strategies, inter-agent context sharing, and fallback behaviors affect susceptibility to adversarial prompting. We introduce Dharma, a diagnostic measure that helps identify weak links within multi-agent pipelines. Using SafeAgents, we conduct a comprehensive study across five widely adopted multi-agent architectures (centralized, decentralized, and hybrid variants) on four datasets spanning web tasks, tool use, and code generation. Our findings reveal that common design patterns carry significant vulnerabilities. For example, centralized systems that delegate only atomic instructions to sub-agents obscure harmful objectives, reducing robustness. Our results highlight the need for security-aware design in MAS. Link to code is https://github.com/microsoft/SafeAgents

</details>
